Synthesis Subset of EVODEX-E

This table shows a subset of EVODEX-E operators used for product prediction tasks such as pathway synthesis. The subset was created by selecting EVODEX-P entries that involve only a single substrate and a single product, and deriving EVODEX-E from those. This allows for mechanistically plausible product predictions without introducing additional substrates or cofactors.
